 THERA GĀTHĀ  
 Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa  
 Sīhānaṃ va nadantānaṃ dāṭhīnaṃ girigabbhare 
 suṇātha bhāvitattānaṃ gāthā attupanāyikā     Th       
 yathānāmā yathāgottā yathādhammavihārino 
 yathādhimuttā sappaññā vihariṃsu atanditā     Th       
 tattha tattha vipassitvā phusitvā accutaṃ padaṃ 
 katantaṃ paccavekkhantā imaṃ atthaṃ abhāsisuṃ     Th       
 EKANIPĀTO  
 Channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā  vassa deva yathāsukhaṃ  
 cittaṃ me susamāhitaṃ vimuttaṃ  ātāpī viharāmi  vassa 
 devā ti     Th      
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Subhūti thero gātham abhāsitthā ti  
 Upasanto uparato mantabhāṇī anuddhato 
 dhunāti pāpake dhamme dumapattaṃ va māluto ti     Th      
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Mahākoṭṭhikathero gātham 
 abhāsittha  
  
                                                                          INTRODUCTORY STANZAS     atthupanāyikā A  attup  C  atthūp  D  atthupaṇāsikā B  Comp

    comp          me sā kuṭikā A Da  me kuṭikā BCDb              Mahākoṭṭhikath  A  Mahākoṭiko th  BC  Mahākoṭṭhitath  D

   THERA GĀTHĀ  
 Paññaṃ imaṃ passa tathāgatānaṃ  aggi yathā pajjalito 
 nisīthe 
 ālokadā cakkhudadā bhavanti ye āgatānaṃ vinayanti 
 kaṅkhan ti     Th      
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Kaṅkhārevato thero gātham 
 abhāsittha  
 Sabbhir eva samāsetha paṇḍiteh  atthadassibhi  
 atthaṃ mahantaṃ gambhīraṃ duddasaṃ nipuṇaṃ aṇuṃ 
 dhīrā samadhigacchanti appamattā vicakkhaṇā ti     Th      
 i  s  āyasmā Puṇṇo Mantāniputto thero g a  
 Yo duddamayo damena danto Dabbo santusito vitiṇṇakaṅkho 
 vijitāvi apetabheravo hi Dabbo so parinibbuto ṭhitatto ti     Th      
 i  s  āyasmā Dabbo thero g a  
 Yo Sītavanaṃ upāgā bhikkhu eko santusito samāhitatto 
 vijitāvi apetalomahaṃso rakkhaṃ kāyagatāsatiṃ dhitīmā 
 ti     Th      
 i  s  āyasmā Sītavaniyo thero  
 Yo pānudi maccurājassa senaṃ naḷasetuṃ va sudubbalaṃ 
 mahogho 
 vijitāvi apetabheravo hi danto so parinibbuto ṭhitatto ti     Th      
 i  s  āyasmā Bhalliyo thero  
 Yo duddamayo damena danto vīro santusito vitiṇṇakaṅkho 
 vijitāvi apetalomahaṃso Vīro so parinibbuto ṭhitatto ti     Th      
 Vīro thero  
 Svāgataṃ nāpagataṃ na yidaṃ dummantitaṃ mama  
 saṃvibhattesu dhammesu yaṃ seṭṭhaṃ tad upāgamin ti     Th      
 Pilindavacchathero  
  
                                                                             aggī A  aggi BCD    nisīve A  nisive BC  nisīthe  sometimes nisīve 
 corrected into nisīthe D  nisīthe rattiyaṃ      hi AD  pi B  deest in C    ṭhitatto AD  ṭhitattho BC     upagā ABC  upāgā D    rakkhi AC  rakkhaṃ BD  Then ABCDa agree 
 in reading kāyagatāsati dhitimā  dhimā C   D  rakkhan ti rakkhato 
  rakkhanto   kāyagatāsatin ti kāyārammaṇaṃ satiṃ kāyagatāsatikammaṭṭhānaṃ paribrahaṇavasena avissajjento    In the 
 commentary this stanza is ascribed to the Thera Sambhūta     naḷaṃ corrected into naḷa  A  daḷaṃ B  daḷhaṭṭhaṃ C  nala  D  
 Comp  Suttanip        comp        na dūrāgataṃ A  nā duragataṃ B  nā dūragato C

  instead of apagataṃ  mentioned in the commentary   nāpi duṭṭhu

 EKA NIPĀTO    
 Vihari apekkhaṃ idha vā huraṃ vā yo vedagū samito 
 yatatto 
 sabbesu dhammesu anupalitto lokassa jaññā udayabbayañ 
 cā ti     Th       
  puṇṇamāsathero   
 Vaggo paṭhamo  uddānaṃ  
 Subhūti Koṭṭhiko thero Kaṅkhārevatasubbato 
 Mantāniputto Dabbo ca Sītavaniyo ca Bhalliyo 
 Vīro Pilindavaccho ca Puṇṇamāso tamonudo ti    
 Pāmujjabahulo bhikkhu dhamme buddhappavedite 
 adhigacche padaṃ santaṃ saṃkhārūpasamaṃ sukhan ti     Th       
 Cūlagavaccho thero  
 Paññābalī sīlavatūpapanno samāhito jhānarato satīmā 
 yadatthiyaṃ bhojanaṃ bhuñjamāno kaṅkheta kālaṃ idha 
 vītarāgo ti     Th       
 Mahāgavaccho thero  
 Nīlabbhavaṇṇā rucirā sītavārī sucindharā 
 indagopakasañchannā te selā ramayanti man ti     Th       
 Vanavacchatthero  
 Upajjhāyo maṃ avacāsi ito gacchāmi Sīvaka  
 gāme me vasati kāyo araññaṃ me gato mano 
 semānako pi gacchāmi  n  atthi saṅgo vijānatan ti     Th       
 Vanavacchassa therassa sāmaṇero  
 Pañca chinde pañca jahe pañca c  uttari bhāvaye  
 pañcasaṅgātigo bhikkhu oghatiṇṇo ti vuccatīti     Th       
 Kuṇḍadhāno thero  
 Yathāpi bhaddo ājañño naṅgalāvattanī sikhī 
 gacchati appakasirena  evaṃ rattindivā mama 
 gacchanti appakasirena sukhe laddhe nirāmise ti     Th       
 Belaṭṭhasīso thero

   THERA GĀTHĀ  
 Middhī yadā hoti mahagghaso ca niddāyitā samparivattasāyī 
 mahāvarāho va nivāpapuṭṭho punappunaṃ gabbham upeti 
 mando ti     Th       
 Dāsako thero  
 Ahū buddhassa dāyādo bhikkhu Bhesakaḷāvane  
 kevalaṃ aṭṭhisaññāya aphari paṭhaviṃ imaṃ  
 maññe haṃ kāmarāgaṃ so khippam eva pahīyatīti     Th       
 Siṅgālapitā thero  
 Udakaṃ hi nayanti nettikā  usukārā namayanti tejanaṃ  
 dāruṃ namayanti tacchakā  attānaṃ damayanti subbatā ti     Th       
 Kuḷo thero  
 Maraṇe me bhayaṃ n  atthi  nikantī n  atthi jīvite  
 sandehaṃ nikkhipissāmi sampajāno patissato ti     Th       
 Ajito thero  
 Vaggo dutiyo  uddānaṃ  
 Cūlavaccho Mahāvaccho Vanavaccho ca Sīvako 
 Kuṇḍadhāno ca Belaṭṭhi Dāsako ca tato paraṃ 
 Siṅgālapitiko thero Kuḷo ca Ajito dasā ti    
 Nāhaṃ bhayassa bhāyāmi  satthā no amatassa kovido  
 yattha bhayaṃ nāvatiṭṭhati tena maggena vajanti bhikkhavo ti     Th       
 Nigrodho thero  
 Nīlā sugīvā sikhino morā Kāraṃviyaṃ abhinadanti  
 te sītavātakalitā suttaṃ jhāyaṃ nibodhentīti     Th       
 Cittako thero

 EKA NIPĀTO    
 Ahaṃ kho Veḷugumbasmiṃ bhutvāna madhupāyāsaṃ 
 padakkhiṇaṃ sammasanto khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ 
 sānuṃ paṭigamissāmi vivekaṃ anubrūhayan ti     Th       
 Gosālo thero  
 Anuvassiko pabbajito  passa dhammasudhammataṃ  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti     Th       
 Sugandho thero  
 Obhāsajātaṃ phalagaṃ cittaṃ yassa abhiṇhaso  
 tādisaṃ bhikkhuṃ āsajja Kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasīti     Th       
 Nandiyo thero  
 Sutvā subhāsitaṃ vācaṃ buddhassādiccabandhuno 
 paccavyādhiṃ hi nipuṇaṃ vālaggaṃ usunā yathā ti     Th       
 Abhayo thero  
 Dabbaṃ kusaṃ poṭakilaṃ usīraṃ muñjapabbajaṃ 
 urasā panudahissāmi vivekam anubrūhayan ti     Th       
 Lomasakaṅgiyo thero  
 Kacci no vatthapasuto  kacci no bhūsanārato  
 kacci sīlamayaṃ gandhaṃ tvaṃ vāsi netarā pajā ti     Th       
 Jambugāmikaputto thero  
 Samunnamayam attānaṃ usukāro va tejanaṃ 
 cittaṃ ujuṃ karitvāna avijjaṃ chinda Hāritā ti     Th       
 Hārito thero  
 Ābādhe me samuppanne sati me upapajjatha  
 ābādho me samuppanno  kālo me na ppamajjitun ti     Th       
 Uttiyo thero  
 Vaggo tatiyo  uddānaṃ  
 Nigrodho Cittako thero Gosālatthero Sugandho 
 Nandiyo Abhayo thero thero Lomasakaṅgiyo 
 Jambugāmikaputto ca Hārito Uttiyo isīti

 evaṃ vutto anuvassiko ti vuttaṃ hoti      sacchabyādhiṃ A  saccappādīhi  corrected into  dhīhi  C

   THERA GĀTHĀ  
 Phuṭṭho ḍaṃsehi makasehi araññasmiṃ brahāvane 
 nāgo saṃgāmasīse va sato tatrādhivāsaye ti     Th       
 Gahvaratīriyo bhikkhu  
 Ajaraṃ jīramānena tappamānena nibbutiṃ 
 nimmissaṃ paramaṃ santiṃ yogakkhemaṃ anuttaran 
 ti     Th       
 Suppiyo thero  
 Yathāpi ekaputtasmiṃ piyasmiṃ kusalī siyā  
 evaṃ sabbesu pāṇesu sabbattha kusalo siyā ti     Th       
 Sopāko thero  
 Anāsannavarā etā niccam eva vijānatā  
 gāmā araññam āgamma tato gehaṃ upāvisiṃ 
 tato uṭṭhāya pakkāmiṃ anāmantetvā Posiyo ti     Th       
 Posiyo thero  
 Sukhaṃ sukhattho labhate tad ācaraṃ  kittiñ ca pappoti  
 yas  assa vaḍḍhati 
 yo ariyam aṭṭhaṅgikam añjasaṃ ujuṃ bhāveti maggaṃ 
 amatassa pattiyā ti     Th       
 Sāmaññakāni thero  
 Sādhu sutaṃ sādhu caritakaṃ sādhu sadā aniketavihāro 
 atthapucchanaṃ padakkhiṇakammaṃ etaṃ sāmaññam 
 akiñcanassā ti     Th       
 Kumāputto thero  
 Nānājanapadaṃ yanti vicarantā asaññatā 
 samādhiñ ca virādhenti  kiṃ su raṭṭhaṃcariyā karissati  
 tasmā vineyya sārambhaṃ jhāyeyya apurakkhato ti     Th       
 Kumāputtassa therassa sahāyako thero  
 Yo iddhiyā Sarabhuṃ aṭṭhapesi so Gavampati asito anejo  
 taṃ sabbasaṅgātigataṃ mahāmuniṃ devā namassanti bhavassa pāragun ti     Th       
 Gavampati thero  
 Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho ḍayhamāne va matthake 
 kāmarāgapahānāya sato bhikkhu paribbaje ti     Th       
 Tisso thero

 Vaḍḍhamāno thero  
 Vaggo catuttho  uddānaṃ

 Gavampati Tissatthero Vaḍḍhamāno mahāyaso ti

 nagavivaragato ca jhāyati putto appaṭimassa tādino ti     Th       
 Sirivaḍḍho thero  
 Cāle Upacāle Sīsūpacāle patissatikā nu kho viharatha  
 āgato vo vālaṃ viya vedhīti     Th       
 Khadiravaniyo thero  
 Sumuttiko sumuttiko sāhu sumuttiko mhi tīhi khujjakehi  
 asitāsu mayā naṅgalāsu mayā khuddakuddālāsu mayā  
 yadi pi idham eva idham eva athavāpi alam eva alam eva  
 jhāya Sumaṅgala jhāya Sumaṅgala  appamatto vihara 
 Sumaṅgalā ti     Th       
 Sumaṅgalo thero  
 Mataṃ vā amma rodanti yo vā jīvaṃ na dissati  
 jīvantaṃ maṃ amma dissantī kasmā maṃ amma rodasīti     Th       
 Sānu thero  
 Yathāpi bhaddo ājañño khalitvā patitiṭṭhati 
 evaṃ dassanasampannaṃ sammāsambuddhasāvakan ti     Th       
 Ramaṇīyavihārī thero  
 Saddhāyāhaṃ pabbajito agārasmā anagāriyaṃ  
 sati paññā ca me vuḍḍhā cittañ ca susamāhitaṃ  
 kāmaṃ karassu rūpāni  n  eva maṃ byādhayissasīti     Th       
 Samiddhi thero

   THERA GĀTHĀ  
 Namo te buddhavīr  atthu  vippamutto si sabbadhi  
 tuyh  āpadāne viharaṃ viharāmi anāsavo ti     Th       
 Ujjayo thero  
 Yato ahaṃ pabbajito agārasmā anagāriyaṃ 
 nābhijānāmi saṃkappaṃ anariyaṃ dosasaṃhitan ti     Th       
 Sañjayo thero  
 Vihavihābhinadite sippikābhirutehi ca 
 na me taṃ phandati cittaṃ  ekattanirataṃ hi me     Th       
 Rāmaṇeyyako thero  
 Dharaṇī ca siccati vāti māluto vijjutā carati nabhe  
 upasammanti vitakkā  cittaṃ susamāhitaṃ mamā ti     Th       
 Vimalo thero  
 Vaggo pañcamo  uddānaṃ  
 Sirivaḍḍho Revato thero Sumaṅgalo Sānusavhayo 
 Ramaṇīyavihārī ca Samiddh   Ujjaya Sañjayo 
 Rāmaṇeyyo ca so thero Vimalo ca raṇañjayo ti  
 Vassati devo yathā sugītaṃ  channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā  
 cittaṃ susamāhitañ ca mayhaṃ  atha ce patthayasi pavassa 
 devā ti     Th       
 Godhiko thero

 cittaṃ susamāhitañ ca kāye  atha ce patthayasi pavassa 
 devā ti     Th       
 Subāhu thero

 Uttiyo thero  
 Āsandiṃ kuṭikaṃ katvā ogayha Añjanaṃ vanaṃ 
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti     Th       
 Añjanāvaniyo thero  
 Ko kuṭikāyaṃ  bhikkhu kuṭikāyaṃ vītarāgo susamāhitacitto  
 evaṃ jānāhi āvuso amoghā te kuṭikā katā ti     Th       
 Kuṭivihārī thero  
 Ayam āhu purāṇiyā kuṭi  aññaṃ patthayase navaṃ kuṭiṃ  
 āsaṃ kuṭiyā virājaya  dukkhā bhikkhu puna navā kuṭīti     Th       
 Kuṭivihārī thero  
 Ramaṇīyā me kuṭikā saddhādeyyā manoramā

 evaṃ subhāvitaṃ cittaṃ rāgo na samativijjhati     Th        
 Rādho thero  
 Khīṇā hi mayhaṃ jāti  vusitaṃ jinasāsanaṃ

 yass  atthāya pabbajito agārasmā anagāriyaṃ

 Surādho thero

 Gotamo thero

 na brāhmaṇo bahivaṇṇo  antovaṇṇo hi brāhmaṇo

 TIKANIPĀTO  
 Ayonisuddhiṃ anvesaṃ aggiṃ paricariṃ vane  
 suddhimaggam ajānanto akāsiṃ amaraṃ tapaṃ     Th        
 taṃ sukhena sukhaṃ laddhaṃ  passa dhammasudhammataṃ  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ     Th        
 brahmabandhu pure āsiṃ  idāni kho mhi brāhmaṇo  
 tevijjo nhātako c  amhi sotthiyo c  amhi vedagū ti     Th        
 Aṅgaṇikabhāradvājo thero  
 Pañcāhāhaṃ pabbajito sekho appattamānaso  
 vihāraṃ me paviṭṭhassa cetaso paṇidhī ahū     Th        
 nāsissaṃ na pivissāmi vihārato na nikkhame 
 na pi passaṃ nipātessaṃ taṇhāsalle anūhate     Th        
 tassa mevaṃ viharato passa viriyaparakkamaṃ  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti     Th        
 Paccayo thero  
 Yo pubbe karaṇīyāni pacchā so kātum icchati  
 sukhā so dhaṃsate ṭhānā pacchā cam anutappati     Th        
 yañ hi kayirā tañ hi vade  yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade  
 akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ parijānanti paṇḍitā     Th        
 susukhaṃ vata nibbānaṃ sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ 
 asokaṃ virajaṃ khemaṃ yattha dukkhaṃ nirujjhatīti     Th        
 Bākulathero  
 Sukhañ ce jīvituṃ icche sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā  
 saṃghikaṃ nātimaññeyya cīvaraṃ pānabhojanaṃ     Th        
 sukhañ ce jīvituṃ icche sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā  
 ahimusikasobbhaṃ va sevetha sayanāsanaṃ     Th

 sukhañ ce jīvituṃ icche sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā  
 itarītarena tusseyya ekadhammañ ca bhāvaye ti     Th        
 Dhaniyo thero  
 Atisītaṃ atiuṇhaṃ atisāyam idaṃ ahū  
 iti vissaṭṭhakammante khaṇā accenti māṇave     Th        
 yo ca sītañ ca uṇhañ ca tiṇā bhiyyo na maññati 
 karaṃ purisakiccāni  so sukhā na vihāyati     Th        
 dabbaṃ kusaṃ poṭakilaṃ usīraṃ mañjapabbajaṃ 
 urasā panudahissāmi vivekam anubrūhayan ti     Th        
 Mātaṅgaputto thero  
 Ye cittakathī bahussutā samaṇā Pāṭaliputtavāsino 
 tes  aññataro yam āyuvā dvāre tiṭṭhati Khujjasobhito     Th        
 ye cittakathī bahussutā samaṇā Pāṭaliputtavāsino 
 tes  aññataro yam āyuvā dvāre tiṭṭhati māluterito     Th        
 suyuddhena suyiṭṭhena saṃgāmavijayena ca 
 brahmacariyānuciṇṇena evāyaṃ sukham edhati     Th        
 Khujjasobhito thero  
 Yo dha koci manussesu parapāṇāni hiṃsati  
 asmā lokā paramhā ca ubhayā dhaṃsate naro     Th        
 yo ca mettena cittena sabbapāṇ  ānukampati  
 bahuṃ hi so pasavati puññaṃ tādisako naro     Th        
 subhāsitassa sikkhetha samaṇupāsanassa ca 
 ekāsanassa ca raho cittavūpasamassa cā ti     Th        
 Vāraṇathero  
 Eko pi saddho medhāvī asaddhān  idha ñātinaṃ 
 dhammaṭṭho sīlasampanno hoti atthāya bandhunaṃ     Th        
 niggayha anukampāya coditā ñātayo mayā 
 ñātibandhavapemena kāraṃ katvāna bhikkhusu     Th        
 te abbhatītā kālakatā pattā te tidivaṃ sukhaṃ  
 bhātaro mayhaṃ mātā ca modanti kāmakāmino ti     Th        
 Passikathero  
 Kālāpabbaṅgasaṃkāso kiso dhamanisantato 
 mattaññu annapānamhi adīnamanaso naro    Th

  CATUKKANIPĀTO   
 Alaṃkatā suvasanā mālinī candanussadā 
 majjhe mahāpathe nārī turiye naccati naṭṭakī     Th        
 piṇḍikāya paviṭṭho haṃ gacchanto naṃ udikkhisaṃ 
 alaṃkataṃ suvasanaṃ maccupāsaṃ va oḍḍitaṃ     Th        
 tato me manasīkāro yoniso udapajjatha  
 ādīnavo pāturahū  nibbidā samatiṭṭhata     Th        
 tato cittaṃ vimucci me  passa dhammasudhammataṃ  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti     Th        
 Nāgasamālathero  
 Ahaṃ middhena pakato vihārā upanikkhamiṃ  
 caṅkamaṃ abhirūhanto tath  eva papatiṃ chamā     Th        
 gattāni parimajjitvā puna pāruyha caṅkamaṃ 
 caṅkame caṅkamiṃ so haṃ ajjhattaṃ susamāhito     Th        
 tato me                               Th            
 Bhagu thero  
 Pare ca na vijānanti mayam ettha yamāmase  
 ye ca tattha vijānanti  tato sammanti medhagā     Th        
 yadā ca avijānantā iriyanty amarā viyā  
 vijānanti ca ye dhammaṃ āturesu anāturā     Th        
 yaṃ kiñci sithilaṃ kammaṃ saṃkiliṭṭhañ ca yaṃ vataṃ 
 saṃkassaraṃ brahmacariyaṃ  na taṃ hoti mahapphalaṃ     Th        
 yassa sabrahmacārīsu gāravo n  ūpalabbhati  
 ārakā hoti saddhammā nabhaṃ puthaviyā yathā ti     Th        
 Sabhiyo thero  
 Dhir atthu pūre duggandhe Mārapakkhe avassute  
 nava sotāni te kāye yāni sandanti sabbadā     Th

 PAÑCA NIPĀTO     
 PAÑCANIPĀTO  
 Bhikkhu sīvathikaṃ gantvā addasaṃ itthim ujjhitaṃ 
 apaviddhaṃ susānasmiṃ khajjantiṃ kimihī phuṭaṃ     Th        
 yaṃ hi eke jigucchanti mataṃ disvāna pāpakaṃ  
 kāmarāgo pāturahū  andho va savatī ahuṃ     Th        
 oraṃ odanapākamhā tamhā ṭhānā apakkamiṃ  
 satimā sampajāno haṃ ekamantaṃ upāvisiṃ     Th        
 tato me                              Th            
 Rājadatto thero  
 Ayoge yuñjam attānaṃ puriso kiccam icchato 
 caraṃ ce nādhigaccheyya  taṃ me dubbhagalakkhaṇaṃ  
           
 abbūḷhaṃ aghataṃ vijitaṃ ekañ ce ossajjeyya kalī va siyā  
 sabbāni pi ce ossajjeyya andho va siyā samavisamassa 
 adassanato     Th        
 yañ hi kayirā                  Th        
 yathāpi ruciraṃ pupphaṃ vaṇṇavantaṃ agandhakaṃ  
 evaṃ subhāsitā vācā aphalā hoti akubbato     Th        
 yathāpi ruciraṃ pupphaṃ vaṇṇavantaṃ sagandhakaṃ 
 evaṃ subhāsitā vācā saphalā hoti sakubbato ti     Th        
 Subhūto thero

    THERA GĀTHĀ  
 Vassati devo yathā sugītaṃ  channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā  
 tassaṃ viharāmi vūpasanto  atha ce patthayasi pavassa 
 deva     Th        
 vassati devo yathā sugītaṃ  channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā  
 tassaṃ viharāmi santacitto   pa   tassaṃ viharāmi vītarāgo       vītadoso       vītamoho  atha ce patthayasi

 Girimānando thero  
 Yaṃ patthayāno dhammesu upajjhāyo anuggahi 
 amataṃ abhikaṅkhantaṃ  kataṃ kattabbakaṃ mayā     Th        
 anuppatto sacchikato sayaṃ dhammo anītiho  
 visuddhañāṇo nikkhaṅkho byākaromi tav  antike     Th        
 pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi  dibbacakkhuṃ visodhitaṃ  
 sadattho me anuppatto  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ     Th        
 appamattassa me sikkhā sussutā tava sāsane  
 sabbe me āsavā khīṇā  n  atthi dāni punabbhavo     Th        
 anusāsi maṃ ariyavatā  anukampī anuggahi  
 amogho tuyham ovādo  antevāsi mhi sikkhito ti     Th        
 Sumano thero  
 Sādhu hi kira me mātā patodaṃ upadaṃsayi  
 yassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā anusiṭṭho janettiyā 
 āraddhaviriyo pahitatto patto sambodhim uttamaṃ     Th        
 arahā dakkhiṇeyyo mhi tevijjo amataddaso  
 jitvā Namucino senaṃ viharāmi anāsavo     Th        
 ajjhattañ ca bahiddhā ca ye me vijjiṃsu āsavā 
 sabbe asesā ucchinnā na ca uppajjare puna     Th        
 visāradā kho bhaginī etaṃ atthaṃ abhāsayi  
 api hā nūna mayi pi vanatho te na vijjati     Th        
 pariyantakataṃ dukkhaṃ  antimo yaṃ samussayo 
 jātimaraṇasaṃsāro  n  atthi dāni punabbhavo ti     Th

 gaṇhe haṃ sabbalokassa niccaṃ kāyagatāsatiṃ     Th        
 ye maṃ rūpena pāmiṃsu ye ca ghosena anvagū 
 chandarāgavasūpetā na maṃ jānanti te janā     Th

 atīva phāsu bhavati ekassa vasato vane     Th        
 handa eko gamissāmi araññaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ

 supupphite Sītavane sītale girikandare

 avaṇṇañ ca akittiñ ca dussīlo labhate naro

 ādi sīlaṃ patiṭṭhā ca kalyāṇānañ ca mātukaṃ

 nābhijānāmi saṃkappaṃ anariyaṃ dosasaṃhitaṃ     Th        
 ime haññantu vajjhantu dukkhaṃ pappontu pāṇino 
 saṃkappaṃ nābhijānāmi imasmiṃ dīghamantare     Th        
 mettañ ca abhijānāmi appamāṇaṃ subhāvitaṃ 
 anupubbaṃ paricitaṃ yathā buddhena desitaṃ     Th        
 sabbamitto sabbasakho sabbabhūtānukampako 
 mettaṃ cittañ ca bhāvemi abyāpajjharato sadā     Th        
 asaṃhīraṃ asaṃkuppaṃ cittaṃ āmodayām  ahaṃ  
 brahmavihāraṃ bhāvemi akāpurisasevitaṃ     Th        
 avitakkaṃ samāpanno sammāsambuddhasāvako 
 ariyena tuṇhibhāvena upeto hoti tāvade     Th        
 yathāpi pabbato selo acalo suppatiṭṭhito  
 evaṃ mohakkhayā bhikkhu pabbato va na vedhati     Th        
 anaṅgaṇassa posassa niccaṃ sucigavesino 
 vālaggamattaṃ pāpassa abbhāmattaṃ va khāyati     Th        
 nagaraṃ yathā paccantaṃ guttaṃ santarabāhiraṃ  
 evaṃ gopetha attānaṃ  khaṇo ve mā upaccagā     Th        
 nābhinandāmi                      Th

 sampādeth  appamādena  esā me anusāsanī  
 handāhaṃ parinibbissaṃ  vippamutto mhi sabbadhīti     Th        
 Revato thero  
 Yathāpi bhaddo ājañño dhure yutto dhurassaho 
 mathito atibhārena saṃyugaṃ nātivattati     Th        
 evaṃ paññāya ye tittā samuddo vārinā yathā 
 na pare atimaññanti  ariyadhammo va pāṇinaṃ     Th

 virāgo desito dhammo anupādāya sabbaso     Th

    THERA GĀTHĀ  
 sabbasaṃyojanātītaṃ vanā nibbanam āgataṃ 
 kāmehi nikkhammarataṃ muttaselā va kañcanaṃ     Th        
 sa ve accantarucī nāgo Himavāvaññe siluccaye  
 sabbesaṃ nāganāmānaṃ saccanāmo anuttaro     Th        
 nāgaṃ vo kittayissāmi  na hi āguṃ karoti so  
 soraccaṃ avihiṃsā ca pādā nāgassa te duve     Th        
 sati ca sampajaññañ ca caraṇā nāgassa te pare  
 saddhāhattho mahānāgo  upekkhāsetadantavā     Th        
 sati gīvā  siro paññā  vīmaṃsā dhammacintanā  
 dhammakucchi  samāvāso  viveko tassa vāladhi     Th        
 so jhāyī assāsarato ajjhattaṃ susamāhito  
 gacchaṃ samāhito nāgo  ṭhito nāgo samāhito           
 sayaṃ samāhito nāgo  nisinno pi samāhito

 bhuñjati anavajjāni  sāvajjāni na bhuñjati  
 ghāsaṃ acchādanaṃ laddhā sannidhiṃ parivajjayaṃ     Th

 yena yen  eva gacchati anapekkho va gacchati     Th

 tath  eva ca loke jāto buddho loke viharati

 VĪSATINIPĀTO  
 Yaññatthaṃ vā dhanatthaṃ vā ye hanāma mayaṃ pure 
 avasesaṃ bhayaṃ hoti  vedhanti vilapanti ca     Th        
 tassa te n  atthi bhītattaṃ  bhiyyo vaṇṇo pasīdati  
 kasmā na paridevesi evarūpe mahabbhaye     Th        
 n  atthi cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ anapekkhassa gāmaṇi  
 atikkantā bhayā sabbe khīṇasaṃyojanassa ve     Th        
 khīṇāya bhavanettiyā diṭṭhe dhamme yathātathe 
 na bhayaṃ maraṇe hoti bhāranikkhepane yathā     Th        
 suciṇṇaṃ brahmacariyaṃ me  maggo cāpi subhāvito  
 maraṇe me bhayaṃ n  atthi rogānam iva saṃkhaye     Th        
 suciṇṇaṃ brahmacariyaṃ me  maggo cāpi subhāvito  
 nirassādā bhavā diṭṭhā  visaṃ pitvāna chaḍḍitaṃ     Th        
 pāragū anupādāno katakicco anāsavo 
 tuṭṭho āyukkhayā hoti mutto āghātanā yathā     Th        
 uttamaṃ dhammataṃ patto sabbaloke anatthiko 
 ādittā va gharā mutto maraṇasmiṃ na socati     Th        
 yad atthi saṃgataṃ kiñci bhavo ca yattha labbhati  
 sabbaṃ anissaraṃ etaṃ  iti vuttaṃ mahesinā     Th        
 yo taṃ tathā pajānāti yathā buddhena desitaṃ  
 na gaṇhati bhavaṃ kiñci sutattaṃ va ayoguḷaṃ     Th        
 na me hoti ahosin ti  bhavissan ti na hoti me  
 saṃkhārā vibhavissanti  tattha kā paridevanā     Th        
 suddhaṃ dhammasamuppādaṃ suddhaṃ saṃkhārasantatiṃ 
 passantassa yathābhūtaṃ na bhayaṃ hoti gāmaṇi     Th        
 tiṇakaṭṭhasamaṃ lokaṃ yadā paññāya passati 
 mamattaṃ so asaṃvindaṃ n  atthi me ti na socati     Th

 anissaraṇadassāvī gandhe ce paṭisevati

 ratto rāgādhikaraṇaṃ vividhaṃ vindate dukhaṃ     Th        
 manañ c  etehi dhammehi yo na sakkoti rakkhituṃ

 alaṃ bālassa mohāya no ca pāragavesino     Th        
 añjanī va navā cittā pūtikāyo alaṃkato

 passāmi loke sadhane manusse  laddhāna vittaṃ na dadanti

 pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā Anuruddho va jhāyati     Th        
 sameto naccagītehi sammaṭāḷappabodhano 
 na tena suddhiṃ ajjhagamā Mārassa visaye rato     Th        
 etañ ca samatikkamma rato buddhassa sāsane 
 sabboghaṃ samatikkamma Anuruddho va jhāyati     Th        
 rūpā saddā rasā gandhā phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā 
 ete ca samatikkamma Anuruddho va jhāyati     Th        
 piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto eko adutiyo muni 
 esati paṃsukūlāni Anuruddho anāsavo     Th        
 vicini aggahī dhovi rajayī dhārayī muni 
 paṃsukūlāni matimā Anuruddho anāsavo     Th        
 mahiccho ca asantuṭṭho saṃsaṭṭho yo ca uddhato  
 tassa dhammā ime honti pāpakā saṃkilesikā     Th        
 sato ca hoti appiccho santuṭṭho avighātavā 
 pavivekarato vitto niccam āraddhavīriyo     Th

 anāsavo ca so hoti  iti vuttaṃ mahesinā     Th

 manomayena kāyena iddhiyā upasaṃkami     Th

 nippapañcarato buddho nippapañcam adesayi     Th

 tisso vijjā anuppattā  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ     Th

 pañcavīsati vassāni yato middhaṃ samūhataṃ     Th

 pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi yattha me vusitaṃ pure

 sattakkhattuṃ manussindo ahaṃ rajjam akārayiṃ

 Anuruddho thero  
 Samaṇassa ahū cintā pupphitamhi mahāvane 
 ekaggassa nisinnassa pavivittassa jhāyino     Th

 VĪSATI NIPĀTO     
 jīvitānaṃ parikkhāre bhesajje atha paccaye 
 na bāḷhaṃ ussukā āsuṃ yathā te āsavakkhaye     Th        
 araññe rukkhamūlesu kandarāsu guhāsu ca 
 vivekaṃ anubrūhantā vihiṃsu tapparāyanā     Th        
 nīcaniviṭṭhā subharā mudū atthaddhamānasā 
 abyāsekā amukharā atthacintāvasānugā     Th        
 tato pāsādikaṃ āsi gataṃ bhuttaṃ nisevitaṃ  
 siniddhā teladhārā va ahosi iriyāpatho     Th        
 sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā mahājhāyī mahāhitā 
 nibbutā dāni te therā  parittā dāni tādisā     Th        
 kusalānañ ca dhammānaṃ paññāya ca parikkhayā 
 sabbākāravarūpetaṃ lujjate jinasāsanaṃ     Th        
 pāpakānañ ca dhammānaṃ kilesānañ ca yo utu 
 upaṭṭhitāvivekāya ye ca saddhammasesakā    Th        
 te kilesā pavaḍḍhantā āvisanti bahuṃ janaṃ  
 kīḷanti maññe bālehi ummattehi va rakkhasā     Th        
 kileseh  ābhibhūtā te tena tena vidhāvitā 
 narā kilesavatthūsu sayaṃgāhe va ghosite     Th        
 pariccajitvā saddhammaṃ aññamaññehi bhaṇḍare  
 diṭṭhigatāni anventā idaṃ seyyo ti maññare     Th        
 dhanañ ca puttaṃ bhariyañ ca chaḍḍayitvāna niggatā 
 kaṭacchubhikkhahetū pi akiccāni nisevare     Th        
 udarāvadehakaṃ bhutvā sayant  uttānaseyyakā  
 kathā vadenti paṭibuddhā yā kathā satthu garahitā     Th        
 sabbakārukasippāni cittikatvāna sikkhare  
 avūpasantā ajjhattaṃ sāmaññattho ti acchati     Th        
 mattikaṃ telaṃ cuṇṇañ ca udakāsanabhojanaṃ 
 gihīnaṃ upanāmenti ākaṅkhantā bahuttaraṃ     Th        
 dantapoṇaṃ kapiṭṭhañ ca pupphakhādaniyāni ca 
 piṇḍapāte ca sampanne ambe āmalakāni ca     Th        
 bhesajjesu yathā vejjā  kiccākicce yathā gihī  
 gaṇikā va vibhūsāyaṃ  issare khattiyā yathā

 nekatikā vañcanikā kūṭasakkhī avāṭukā 
 bahūhi parikappehi āmisaṃ paribhuñjare     Th        
 lesakappe pariyāye parikappe nudhāvitā 
 jīvikatthā upāyena saṃkaḍḍhanti bahuṃ dhanaṃ     Th        
 upaṭṭhapenti parisaṃ kammato no ca dhammato

 saṃghalābhassa bhaṇḍanti saṃghato paribāhirā  
 paralābhopajīvantā ahirikā va na lajjare     Th        
 nānuyuttā tathā eke muṇḍā saṃghāṭipārutā 
 sambhāvanaṃ yev  icchanti lābhasakkāramucchitā     Th

 kiñcāpi pacchimo kālo phuseyya amataṃ padaṃ     Th

 brāhmaṇo parinibbāyi isi khīṇapunabbhavo ti     Th

 TIṂSANIPĀTO  
 Pāsādike bahū disvā bhāvitatte susaṃvute 
 isi Paṇḍarasagotto apucchi Phussasavhayaṃ     Th        
 kiṃchandā kimadhippāyā kimākappā bhavissare 
 anāgatamhi kālamhi  taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito     Th        
 suṇohi vacanaṃ mayhaṃ isi Paṇḍarasavhaya  
 sakkaccaṃ upadhārehi  ācikkhissāmy anāgataṃ     Th        
 kodhanā upanāhī ca makkhī thambhī saṭhā bahū 
 issukī nānāvādā ca bhavissanti anāgate    Th        
 aññātamānino dhamme gambhīre tīragocarā 
 lahukā agarū dhamme aññamaññam agāravā     Th        
 bahū ādīnavā loke uppajjissanti nāgate  
 sudesitaṃ imaṃ dhammaṃ kilisissanti dummati     Th        
 guṇahīnāpi saṃghamhi voharanti visāradā 
 balavanto bhavissanti mukharā assutāvino     Th        
 guṇavanto pi saṃghamhi voharantā yathatthato 
 dubbalā te bhavissanti hirimanā anatthikā     Th        
 rajataṃ jātarūpañ ca khettaṃ vatthuṃ ajeḷakaṃ 
 dāsīdāsañ ca dummedhā sādiyissanti nāgate     Th        
 ujjhānasaññino bālā sīlesu asamāhitā 
 unnaḷā vicarissanti kalahābhiratā magā     Th        
 uddhatā ca bhavissanti nīlacīvarapārutā  
 kuhā thaddhā lapā siṅgī carissanty ariyā viya     Th        
 telasaṇhehi kesehi capalā añjanakkhikā 
 rathiyāya gamissanti dantavaṇṇakapārutā     Th        
 ajegucchaṃ vimuttehi surattaṃ arahaddhajaṃ 
 jigucchissanti kāsāvaṃ odātesu samucchitā     Th        
 lābhakāmā bhavissanti kusītā hīnavīriyā  
 kicchantā vanapattāni gāmantesu vasissare     Th

    THERA GĀTHĀ  
 ye ye lābhaṃ labhissanti micchājīvaratā sadā  
 te te ca anusikkhantā bhajissanti asaṃyatā     Th        
 ye ye alābhino lābhaṃ  na te pujjā bhavissare  
 supesale pi te dhīre sevissanti na te tadā     Th        
 milakkhurajanaṃ rattaṃ garahantā sakaṃ dhajaṃ 
 titthiyānaṃ dhajaṃ keci dhāressanty avadātakaṃ     Th        
 agāravo ca kāsāve tadā tesaṃ bhavissati  
 paṭisaṃkhā ca kāsāve bhikkhūnaṃ na bhavissati     Th        
 abhibhūtassa dukkhena sallaviddhassa ruppato 
 paṭisaṃkhā mahāghorā nāgassāsi acintiyā     Th        
 chaddanto hi tadā disvā surattaṃ arahaddhajaṃ 
 tāvad eva bhaṇī gāthā gajo atthopasañhitā     Th        
 anikkasāvo kāsāvaṃ yo vatthaṃ paridahissati 
 apeto damasaccena  na so kāsāvam arahati     Th        
 yo ca vantakasāv  assa sīlesu susamāhito 
 upeto damasaccena  sa ve kāsāvam arahati     Th        
 vipannasīlo dummedho pākaṭo kāmakāriyo 
 vibbhantacitto nissukko  na so kāsāvam arahati     Th        
 yo ca sīlena sampanno vītarāgo samāhito 
 odātamanasaṃkappo  sa ve kāsāvam arahati     Th        
 uddhato unnaḷo bālo sīlaṃ yassa na vijjati  
 odātakaṃ arahati  kāsāvaṃ kiṃ karissati     Th        
 bhikkhū ca bhikkhuniyo ca duṭṭhacittā anādarā 
 tādīnaṃ mettacittānaṃ niggaṇhissanti nāgate     Th        
 sikkhāpentāpi therehi bālā cīvaradhāraṇaṃ 
 na suṇissanti dummedhā pākaṭā kāmakāriyā     Th        
 te tathā sikkhitā bālā aññamaññaṃ agāravā 
 nādiyissant  upajjhāye khaluṅko viya sārathiṃ     Th        
 evaṃ anāgataddhānaṃ paṭipatti bhavissati 
 bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnañ ca patte kālamhi pacchime     Th        
 purā āgacchate etaṃ anāgataṃ mahabbhayaṃ 
 subbacā hotha sakhilā aññamaññaṃ sagāravā     Th        
 mettacittā kāruṇikā hotha sīle susaṃvutā 
 āraddhaviriyā pahitattā niccaṃ daḷhaparakkamā     Th

 Dabbo cirarattaṃ samāhito akuhako nipako apihālu 
 santaṃ padam ajjhagamā muni  paṭiccaparinibbuto kaṅkhati kālaṃ     Th         
 mānaṃ pajahassu Gotama mānapathañ ca jahassu asesaṃ  
 mānapathamhi samucchito vippaṭisārī hutvā cirarattaṃ     Th         
 makkhena makkhitā pajā mānahatā nirayaṃ patanti  
 socanti janā cirarattaṃ mānahatā nirayaṃ upapannā     Th         
 na hi socati bhikkhu kadāci maggajino sammā paṭipanno

 tathattaṃ     Th

 kamarāgena ḍayhāmi  cittaṃ me pariḍayhati  
 sādhu nibbāpanaṃ brūhi anukampāya Gotama     Th         
 saññāya vipariyesā cittan te pariḍayhati  
 nimittaṃ parivajjehi subhaṃ rāgūpasaṃhitaṃ     Th

 sati kāyagatā ty atthu  nibbidābahulo bhava     Th

 tato mānābhisamayā upasanto carissasi     Th         
 tam eva vācaṃ bhāseyya yāy  attānaṃ na tāpaye 
 pare ca na vihiṃseyya  sā ve vācā subhāsitā     Th         
 piyavācam eva bhāseyya yā vācā paṭinanditā 
 yaṃ anādāya pāpāni paresaṃ bhāsate piyaṃ     Th         
 saccaṃ ve amatā vācā  esa dhammo sanantano  
 sacce atthe ca dhamme ca āhu santo paṭiṭṭhitā     Th         
 yaṃ buddho bhāsatī vācaṃ khemaṃ nibbānapattiyā 
 dukkhass  antakiriyāya  sa ve vācānam uttamā     Th         
 gambhīrapañño mehāvī maggāmaggassa kovido

 Koṇḍañño buddhadāyādo pāde vandati satthuno     Th         
 nāgassa passe āsīnaṃ muniṃ dukkhassa pāraguṃ 
 sāvakā pariyupāsanti tevijjā maccuhāyino     Th         
 cetasā anupariyeti Moggallāno mahiddhiko 
 cittaṃ nesaṃ samanvesaṃ vippamuttaṃ nirūpadhiṃ     Th         
 evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ muniṃ dukkhassa pāraguṃ 
 anekākārasampannaṃ payirupāsanti Gotamaṃ     Th         
 cando yathā vigatavalāhake nabhe virocati vītamalo va 
 bhānumā  
 evam pi Aṅgīrasa tvaṃ mahāmuni atirocasī yasasā sabbalokaṃ     Th         
 kāveyyamattā vicarimha pubbe gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ  
  ath  addasāmi sambuddhaṃ  sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ     Th         
 so me dhammam adesesi muni dukkhassa pāragū  
 dhammaṃ sutvā pasīdimha  saddhā no udapajjatha     Th         
 tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā khandhe āyatanāni ca 
 dhātuyo ca viditvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ     Th         
 bahūnaṃ vata atthāya uppajjanti tathāgatā 
 itthīnaṃ purisānañ ca ye te sāsanakārakā     Th         
 tesaṃ kho vata atthāya bodhiṃ ajjhagamā muni 
 bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnañ ca ye niyāmagataṃdasā     Th         
 sudesitā cakkhumatā buddhenādiccabandhunā 
 cattāri ariyasaccāni anukampāya pāṇinaṃ     Th         
 dukkhaṃ dukkhasamuppādaṃ dukkhassa ca atikkamaṃ 
 ariyaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ dukkhūpasamagāminaṃ     Th         
 evam ete tathā vuttā  diṭṭhā me te yathātathā  
 sadattho me anuppatto  kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ     Th         
 svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike  
 saṃvibhattesu dhammesu yaṃ seṭṭhaṃ tad upāgamiṃ     Th         
 abhiññāpāramippatto sotadhātuvisodhito 
 tevijjo iddhippatto mhi cetopariyakovido     Th

 vicikicchānaṃ chetvā

 Nigrodhakappo iti tassa nāmaṃ tayā kataṃ bhagavā 
 brāhmaṇassa  
 so taṃ namassaṃ acari mutyapekho āraddhaviriyo daḷhadhammadassī     Th         
 taṃ sāvakaṃ Sakka mayam pi sabbe aññātum icchāma samantacakkhu  
 samavaṭṭhitā no savanāya sotaṃ  tuvaṃ nu satthā tvam 
 anuttaro si     Th         
 chind  eva no vicikicchaṃ  brūhi me taṃ  parinibbutaṃ 
 vedaya bhūripañña  
 majjheva no bhāsa samantacakkhu Sakko va devāna sahassanetto     Th         
 ye keci gandhā idha mohamaggā aññāṇapakkhā vicikicchaṭṭhānā

 eva maññe

     THERA GĀTHĀ  
 bindussarena suvikappitena  sabbeva te ujjugatā suṇoma     Th         
 pahīnajātimaraṇaṃ asesaṃ niggayha dhonaṃ vadessāmi 
 dhammaṃ  
 na kāmakāro hi puthujjanānaṃ  saṃkheyyakāro va tathāgatānaṃ     Th

 ayam añjali pacchimo suppaṇāmito  mā mohayi jānam 
 anomapañña     Th

 yadatthiyaṃ brahmacariyaṃ acāri Kappāyano kacci ssa 
 taṃ amoghaṃ

 dīgharattānusayitaṃ
